monetary_system = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
		}

		localization_key = gold_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}

		localization_key = bimetallism_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}

		localization_key = silver_good
	}
}
monetary_system_name = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
		}

		localization_key = gold_name
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}

		localization_key = bimetallism_name
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}

		localization_key = silver_name
	}
}

monetary_system_partiel = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
			}
		}

		localization_key = gold_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}

		localization_key = silver_good
	}
}

	#dinar
	dinar_currency_accumulation = {
		type = country
		log_loc_errors = no

		text = {
			trigger = {
				var:stockpiling_dinar_c_var_2 > 0
			}

			localization_key = green_arow_bellow
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				var:stockpiling_dinar_c_var_2 < 0
			}

			localization_key = red_arow_bellow
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				var:stockpiling_dinar_c_var_2 = 0
			}

			localization_key = yellow_arrow
		}
	}

law_monetary_policy	= {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
		}

		localization_key = law_no_monetary_policy
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_war_economy
		}

		localization_key = law_war_economy
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:revaluation_on = 1
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_100

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_25

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_50

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_75

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_100

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_25

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_50

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_75

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_100

	}
}
law_monetary_policy_texture	= {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
		}

		localization_key = law_no_monetary_policy_texture
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_war_economy
		}

		localization_key = law_war_economy_texture
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
				var:revaluation_on = 1
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_texture

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_100
				var:devaluation_on = 1
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_texture
	}
}

country_credit_rating_texture = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating >= 499
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}

		localization_key = AAA
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 499
			#country_credit_rating >= 375
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		}

		localization_key = AA
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 375
			#country_credit_rating >= 250
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		}

		localization_key = A
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 250
			#country_credit_rating >= 200
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		}

		localization_key = BBB
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 200
			#country_credit_rating >= 150
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		}

		localization_key = BB
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 150
			#country_credit_rating >= 100
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		}

		localization_key = B
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 100
			#country_credit_rating >= 80
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		}

		localization_key = CCC
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 80
			#country_credit_rating >= 60
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		}

		localization_key = CC
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 60
			#country_credit_rating >= 40
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		}

		localization_key = C
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating < 40
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		}

		localization_key = D
	}
}

modifier_currency_value = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value > global_var:money_value_median
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}

		localization_key = strong_currency
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value < global_var:money_value_median
			money_value > 0.0001
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}

		localization_key = weak_currency
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			money_value < 0.001
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}

		localization_key = extreme_weak_currency
	}
}
